  pass

route-policy RTVOIP
  if (extcommunity rt matches-any 1) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy

route-policy VPN-INT
  if (destination in 1) then
    set community (28513:1281)
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy NORTVOIP
  if (extcommunity rt matches-any 1) then
    drop
  else
    pass
  endif
end-policy

route-policy PEER-LDP
  if (destination in 1410) then
    pass
  endif
end-policy
!
route-policy DUAL_HOMED
  if (community matches-any 1) then
    set local-preference 100
  elseif (community matches-any 2) then
    set local-preference 98
  elseif (community matches-any 3) then
    set local-preference 96
  elseif (community matches-any 4) then
    set local-preference 94
  elseif (community matches-any 5) then
    set local-preference 92
  elseif (community matches-any 6) then
